Located in Atlanta, The High Museum is the leading art museum in the Southeastern United States. Its permanent collection includes modern and contemporary art. The graphics are based on the main building of the museum. Graphic shapes are discovered from it from different point of views, since it looks like a group of small unique shaped buildings.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full\"><img lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>11.11.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"https://www.behance.net/lyneeea5863\">Lyne Ea</a> shared a beautiful editorial design project titled Subliminal. Cognitive sciences bring together a set of scientific disciplines dedicated to the description, explanation and simulation of the mechanisms of human thought. The subliminal revue is interested in many phenomena such as perception, intelligence, language or emotion through the prism of cognitive sciences and the different disciplines that make it up, thus combining a variety of articles offering the reader a less scientific but more open approach.</p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/alfa-bank-ios-app-design-concept\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/image_processing20201026-6574-1ulcm1o.jpg\" width=\"1600\" height=\"1199\" alt=\"Alfa Bank iOS App Design Concept\" title=\"Alfa Bank iOS App Design Concept\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>11.10.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>We are sharing the an iOS concept of the Alfa Bank on iOS designed by <a href=\"https://www.behance.net/grinchuk_m\">Mihail Grinchuk</a>, a digital product designer based on Saint Petersburg, Russian Federation. This is officially our first case study sharing mockups with the new iPhone 12 Pro (Yay!). Back to the case study, first of all, it's a nice redesign. Most of us will be familiar with some of the visual approach since it's somehow a standard now in financial technologies. You know what I mean if you think of 'dark mode, graphs, cards at the top of the layout and etc. One cool touch is the introduction of Skewmorphism-style on some of the UI components. It's a simple and clean design, it's probably a common interface for most users nowadays who are getting used to social media platforms and beyond.</p>\n\n<ul><li><a Book","link":"http://feedproxy.google.com/~r/abduzeedo/~3/jHtP9Dm3sGg/airports-aerial-photo-book","description":"AIRPORTS - an Aerial Photo Book\n            <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/airports-aerial-photo-book\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/pasted%20image%200_0.png\" width=\"1200\" height=\"1600\" alt=\"AIRPORTS - an Aerial Photo Book\" title=\"AIRPORTS - an Aerial Photo Book\" typeof=\"foaf:Image\" /></a>\n</div>\n      <a title=\"View user profile.\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/aoirostudio\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>11.09.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>We would like to share another photo book titled 'Airports' by the mighty <a href=\"http://tomhegen.de/\">Tom Hegen</a> who is an aerial photographer based in Munich, Germany. We have featured his work many times on abdz, I think why his work is quite unique for two things. One, I do enjoy the fact that Tom actually takes 'aerial photography' from an actual helicopter ride, not just a 'drone shot'. It makes it even more challenging somehow. Two, the subjects that drive Tom's motivation are different from what we usually see on our social feeds. Following this never-ending pandemic, Tom has released this incredible photo book about 'AIRPORTS'. It's a 176 pages photo book with 100 photographs, make sure to check <a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/tomhegen/airports-aerial-photo-book\">his full project on Kickstarter</a>.</p>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/tomhegen/airports-aerial-photo-book\">Support Tom on Kickstarter</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"http://tomhegen.de/\">http://tomhegen.de/</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/tomhegen.de\">https://www.instagram.com/tomhegen.de</a></li>\n</ul><blockquote>AIRPORTS is an aerial photo project by Tom Hegen. During the lockdown time in March, April and May, I took photographs of the largest German Airports and their resting runways. It was a historic moment and a unique opportunity to get these images. The book will be published in a high-quality clothbound hardcover book by renowned German publisher Hatje Cantz.</blockquote>\n\n<p><img           <div class=\"field__item  Image field_image\">  <a href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/learning-blender-3d\"><img src=\"https://abduzeedo.com/sites/default/files/originals/abdz_6.png\" href=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" lang=\"\" about=\"https://abduzeedo.com/profile/abduzeedo\" typeof=\"schema:Person\" property=\"schema:name\" datatype=\"\" class=\"username\" xml:lang=\"\">abduzeedo</a>11.10.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>For the past month or so I started to learn 3D. My tool of choice, <a href=\"https://www.blender.org/\">Blender.</a> I played with Cinema 4D in the past. I think it’s a phenomenal tool, however, I cannot ignore the fact that it is expensive. Well, at least for me, which the purpose right now is learn and have fun, no ROI. I also knew about Blender, but didn’t know how active the community was. So many tutorial videos and resources available for free. It reminded me a bit of the early 2000s when I started the blog with Photoshop tutorials. </p>\n\n<p>Learning a new tool is not easy, but the sense of accomplishment is quite rewarding, even when the result is not that great. I just wanted to share some images I’ve created in the past couple of weekends. If you have feedback, tutorials to share or links, please let me know. You can also see my latest experiments here or on my personal <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/fmsasso/\">Instagram (@fmsasso)</a></p>\n\n<div class=\"full_padding\"><img xml:lang=\"\">AoiroStudio</a>11.08.20\n            <div class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p>My good pal <a href=\"https://www.johan.media/\">Johan Corminboeuf</a> has shared his photographic project on <a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/johan-corminboeuf/shot-on-my-phone-the-book?ref=68viyk\">Kickstarter</a>. A photography book titled: 'Shot on my Phone'. It's a 4-year photography project displaying his photographic journey and his adventures around the World. Now he needs your support to help put this 350+ pages & 6x9in book to realization. This book will include more than 300 pictures, hardcover, sewn binding, and printed in Italy. The book is also available in French and English. In this book, you will find what he calls 'The Series', from the beautiful Swiss mountains all the way to the North countries. I took the liberty to share a sneak peek for you and don't forget to give Johan some love on his <a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/johan-corminboeuf/shot-on-my-phone-the-book?ref=68viyk\">Kickstarter</a>.</p>\n\n<ul><li><a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/johan-corminboeuf/shot-on-my-phone-the-book?ref=68viyk\">Support Johan on Kickstarter</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.johan.media/projets/shot-on-my-phone\">https://www.johan.media/projets/shot-on-my-phone</a></li>\n\t<li><a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/johan.media/\">https://www.instagram.com/johan.media/</a></li>\n</ul><div data-oembed-url=\"https://vimeo.com/407698332\">\n<div style=\"max-width:1440px;margin:auto;\"><!-- You're using demo endpoint of Iframely API commercially. class=\"clearfix text-formatted blog-content field__item  Body Array body\"><p><a href=\"http://www.steldesign.com/\">STEL Design</a> is an industrial design studio based in Santa Barbara, CA, USA and we are taking a look at the design of the <a href=\"https://nomadgoods.com/products/base-station-pro\">NOMAD Base Station Pro</a>. In other words, a full surface wireless charging station where you can charge up to three devices that can be placed anywhere on the actual surface. And as I quote: 'An 18-coil matrix lies beneath a seamless surface for an effortless charging experience.' I really dig the design, it's classy, premium feel and it comes in black. Standing true to the NOMAD brand and users seems to enjoy its design and efficiency. For more information about the product, check out their site at <a href=\"https://nomadgoods.com\">https://nomadgoods.com</a>.</p>\n\n<ul><li>Get your <a
